House Joint Resolution 11 - Introduced


                                 HOUSE JOINT RESOLUTION 

                                 HOUSE JOINT RESOLUTION 
                                 HOUSE JOINT RESOLUTION                                  HOUSE JOINT RESOLUTION                                  BY  NUNN, HAGENOW,
                                     UPMEYER, HIGHFILL,
                                     McKEAN, KAUFMANN,
                                     WILLS, WATTS, FISHER,
                                     FORRISTALL, HEIN,
                                     PETTENGILL, FRY,
                                     ROGERS, BACON, DEYOE,
                                     HOLZ, LANDON, SHEETS,
                                     SALMON, SEXTON, MOORE,
                                     MOMMSEN, MAXWELL,
                                     HUSEMAN, HEARTSILL,
                                     LUNDGREN, R. TAYLOR,
                                     MOHR, PAUSTIAN, SIECK,
                                     GASSMAN, CARLIN,
                                     KLEIN, BAXTER, HOLT,
                                     RIZER, HINSON,
                                     GRASSLEY,
                                     BLOOMINGDALE, and
                                     ZUMBACH

 HOUSE JOINT RESOLUTION

  1 A Joint Resolution calling for an Article V convention in order
  2    to propose amendments to the Constitution of the United
  3    States that impose fiscal restraints, and limit the power
  4    and jurisdiction of the federal government, and requesting
  5    Congress to similarly propose such amendments.
  6 WHEREAS, the founders of the Constitution of the United
  7 States empowered state legislators to be guardians of liberty
  8 against future abuses of power by the federal government; and
  9 WHEREAS, the federal government has created a crushing
 10 national debt through improper and imprudent spending; and
 11 WHEREAS, the federal government has invaded the legitimate
 12 roles of the states through the manipulative process of federal
 13 mandates, most of which are unfunded to a great extent; and
 14 WHEREAS, the federal government has ceased to live under
 15 a proper interpretation of the Constitution of the United
 16 States; and
 17 WHEREAS, it is the solemn duty of the states to protect
 18 the liberty of our people, particularly for the generations
 19 to come, by proposing amendments to the Constitution of the
 20 United States through a convention of the states under Article
 21 V of the Constitution of the United States for the purpose of
 22 restraining these and related abuses of power; NOW THEREFORE,
 23 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE GENERAL ASSEMBLY OF THE STATE OF IOWA:
    TLSB 2105YH (5) 87
    aw/rj

PAG LIN



  1  1    That the Congress of the United States is hereby petitioned
  1  2 to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the United
  1  3 States, for submission to the states for ratification, to
  1  4 impose fiscal restraints on the federal government and limit
  1  5 the federal government's power and jurisdiction; and
  1  6    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That, pursuant to Article V of the
  1  7 Constitution of the United States, the General Assembly, as the
  1  8 legislature of the state of Iowa, joins in the applications of
  1  9 the states of Georgia (SR 736, 2014), Florida (SM 476, 2014),
  1 10 Alaska (HJR 22, 2014), Alabama (HJR 112, 2015), Tennessee
  1 11 (SJR 67, 2016), Indiana (SJR 14, 2016), Oklahoma (SJR 4,
  1 12 2016), and Louisiana (SCR 52, 2016),  for a convention for the
  1 13 specific and exclusive purpose of proposing amendments to the
  1 14 Constitution of the United States limited to the purposes
  1 15 stated therein, provided, however, that the delegates from
  1 16 Iowa to said convention are expressly limited to consideration
  1 17 and support of amendments that impose fiscal restraints on the
  1 18 federal government, and amendments that limit the power and
  1 19 jurisdiction of the federal government, and no amendments on
  1 20 any other topic; and
  1 21    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That it is the express intention of
  1 22 the General Assembly that this application shall be aggregated
  1 23 with the prior and subsequent applications of other states
  1 24 limited to the purposes identified in this application; and
  1 25    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That this application constitutes
  1 26 a continuing application in accordance with Article V of the
  1 27 Constitution of the United States until the legislatures of at
  1 28 least two=thirds of the several states have made applications
  1 29 for a similar convention under Article V, or the General
  1 30 Assembly resolves to withdraw this application; and
  1 31    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That the Secretary of State shall
  1 32 transmit certified copies of this resolution to the President
  1 33 and Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and
  1 34 Clerk of the United States House of Representatives, the
  1 35 presiding officer of each house of the legislature of each of
  2  1 the several states, and to each member of Iowa's congressional
  2  2 delegation.
  2  3                           EXPLANATION
  2  4 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  2  5 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  2  6    This joint resolution constitutes an application requesting
  2  7 the United States Congress to call a constitutional convention
  2  8 in order to propose amendments to the Constitution of the
  2  9 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 10 government and limit the power and jurisdiction of the federal
  2 11 government. The resolution stipulates that Iowa's delegates
  2 12 to such a convention are expressly limited to consideration
  2 13 and support of amendments on those topics. The resolution
  2 14 constitutes a continuing application to call a constitutional
  2 15 convention and states the intention of the General Assembly
  2 16 that the application be aggregated with the prior and
  2 17 subsequent applications of other states limited to the purposes
  2 18 identified in the resolution.
  2 19    The resolution also petitions the Congress of the United
  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.
       LSB 2105YH (5) 87
       aw/rj

                                     WILLS, WATTS, FISHER,

 10 national debt through improper and imprudent spending; and
 11 WHEREAS, the federal government has invaded the legitimate
 12 roles of the states through the manipulative process of federal
 13 mandates, most of which are unfunded to a great extent; and
 14 WHEREAS, the federal government has ceased to live under
 15 a proper interpretation of the Constitution of the United
 16 States; and
 17 WHEREAS, it is the solemn duty of the states to protect
 18 the liberty of our people, particularly for the generations
 19 to come, by proposing amendments to the Constitution of the
 20 United States through a convention of the states under Article
 21 V of the Constitution of the United States for the purpose of
 22 restraining these and related abuses of power; NOW THEREFORE,
 23 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE GENERAL ASSEMBLY OF THE STATE OF IOWA:

PAG LIN



  1  1    That the Congress of the United States is hereby petitioned
  1  2 to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the United
  1  3 States, for submission to the states for ratification, to
  1  4 impose fiscal restraints on the federal government and limit
  1  5 the federal government's power and jurisdiction; and
  1  6    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That, pursuant to Article V of the
  1  7 Constitution of the United States, the General Assembly, as the
  1  8 legislature of the state of Iowa, joins in the applications of
  1  9 the states of Georgia (SR 736, 2014), Florida (SM 476, 2014),
  1 10 Alaska (HJR 22, 2014), Alabama (HJR 112, 2015), Tennessee
  1 11 (SJR 67, 2016), Indiana (SJR 14, 2016), Oklahoma (SJR 4,
  1 12 2016), and Louisiana (SCR 52, 2016),  for a convention for the
  1 13 specific and exclusive purpose of proposing amendments to the
  1 14 Constitution of the United States limited to the purposes
  1 15 stated therein, provided, however, that the delegates from

  1 18 federal government, and amendments that limit the power and
  1 19 jurisdiction of the federal government, and no amendments on
  1 20 any other topic; and
  1 21    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That it is the express intention of
  1 22 the General Assembly that this application shall be aggregated
  1 23 with the prior and subsequent applications of other states
  1 24 limited to the purposes identified in this application; and
  1 25    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That this application constitutes
  1 26 a continuing application in accordance with Article V of the
  1 27 Constitution of the United States until the legislatures of at
  1 28 least two=thirds of the several states have made applications
  1 29 for a similar convention under Article V, or the General
  1 30 Assembly resolves to withdraw this application; and
  1 31    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That the Secretary of State shall
  1 32 transmit certified copies of this resolution to the President
  1 33 and Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and
  1 34 Clerk of the United States House of Representatives, the
  1 35 presiding officer of each house of the legislature of each of
  2  1 the several states, and to each member of Iowa's congressional
  2  2 delegation.
  2  3                           EXPLANATION
  2  4 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  2  5 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  2  6    This joint resolution constitutes an application requesting
  2  7 the United States Congress to call a constitutional convention
  2  8 in order to propose amendments to the Constitution of the
  2  9 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 10 government and limit the power and jurisdiction of the federal
  2 11 government. The resolution stipulates that Iowa's delegates

  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.

 HOUSE JOINT RESOLUTION

  1 A Joint Resolution calling for an Article V convention in order
  2    to propose amendments to the Constitution of the United
  3    States that impose fiscal restraints, and limit the power
  4    and jurisdiction of the federal government, and requesting
  5    Congress to similarly propose such amendments.
  6 WHEREAS, the founders of the Constitution of the United
  7 States empowered state legislators to be guardians of liberty
  8 against future abuses of power by the federal government; and
  9 WHEREAS, the federal government has created a crushing
 10 national debt through improper and imprudent spending; and
 11 WHEREAS, the federal government has invaded the legitimate
 12 roles of the states through the manipulative process of federal
 13 mandates, most of which are unfunded to a great extent; and
 14 WHEREAS, the federal government has ceased to live under
 15 a proper interpretation of the Constitution of the United
 16 States; and
 17 WHEREAS, it is the solemn duty of the states to protect
 18 the liberty of our people, particularly for the generations
 19 to come, by proposing amendments to the Constitution of the
 20 United States through a convention of the states under Article
 21 V of the Constitution of the United States for the purpose of
 22 restraining these and related abuses of power; NOW THEREFORE,
 23 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE GENERAL ASSEMBLY OF THE STATE OF IOWA:
    TLSB 2105YH (5) 87
    aw/rj

PAG LIN



  1  1    That the Congress of the United States is hereby petitioned
  1  2 to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the United
  1  3 States, for submission to the states for ratification, to
  1  4 impose fiscal restraints on the federal government and limit
  1  5 the federal government's power and jurisdiction; and
  1  6    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That, pursuant to Article V of the
  1  7 Constitution of the United States, the General Assembly, as the
  1  8 legislature of the state of Iowa, joins in the applications of
  1  9 the states of Georgia (SR 736, 2014), Florida (SM 476, 2014),
  1 10 Alaska (HJR 22, 2014), Alabama (HJR 112, 2015), Tennessee
  1 11 (SJR 67, 2016), Indiana (SJR 14, 2016), Oklahoma (SJR 4,
  1 12 2016), and Louisiana (SCR 52, 2016),  for a convention for the
  1 13 specific and exclusive purpose of proposing amendments to the
  1 14 Constitution of the United States limited to the purposes
  1 15 stated therein, provided, however, that the delegates from
  1 16 Iowa to said convention are expressly limited to consideration
  1 17 and support of amendments that impose fiscal restraints on the
  1 18 federal government, and amendments that limit the power and
  1 19 jurisdiction of the federal government, and no amendments on
  1 20 any other topic; and
  1 21    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That it is the express intention of
  1 22 the General Assembly that this application shall be aggregated
  1 23 with the prior and subsequent applications of other states
  1 24 limited to the purposes identified in this application; and
  1 25    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That this application constitutes
  1 26 a continuing application in accordance with Article V of the
  1 27 Constitution of the United States until the legislatures of at
  1 28 least two=thirds of the several states have made applications
  1 29 for a similar convention under Article V, or the General
  1 30 Assembly resolves to withdraw this application; and
  1 31    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That the Secretary of State shall
  1 32 transmit certified copies of this resolution to the President
  1 33 and Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and
  1 34 Clerk of the United States House of Representatives, the
  1 35 presiding officer of each house of the legislature of each of
  2  1 the several states, and to each member of Iowa's congressional
  2  2 delegation.
  2  3                           EXPLANATION
  2  4 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  2  5 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  2  6    This joint resolution constitutes an application requesting
  2  7 the United States Congress to call a constitutional convention
  2  8 in order to propose amendments to the Constitution of the
  2  9 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 10 government and limit the power and jurisdiction of the federal
  2 11 government. The resolution stipulates that Iowa's delegates
  2 12 to such a convention are expressly limited to consideration
  2 13 and support of amendments on those topics. The resolution
  2 14 constitutes a continuing application to call a constitutional
  2 15 convention and states the intention of the General Assembly
  2 16 that the application be aggregated with the prior and
  2 17 subsequent applications of other states limited to the purposes
  2 18 identified in the resolution.
  2 19    The resolution also petitions the Congress of the United
  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.

    TLSB 2105YH (5) 87
    aw/rj

PAG LIN



  1  1    That the Congress of the United States is hereby petitioned
  1  2 to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the United
  1  3 States, for submission to the states for ratification, to
  1  4 impose fiscal restraints on the federal government and limit
  1  5 the federal government's power and jurisdiction; and
  1  6    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That, pursuant to Article V of the
  1  7 Constitution of the United States, the General Assembly, as the
  1  8 legislature of the state of Iowa, joins in the applications of
  1  9 the states of Georgia (SR 736, 2014), Florida (SM 476, 2014),
  1 10 Alaska (HJR 22, 2014), Alabama (HJR 112, 2015), Tennessee
  1 11 (SJR 67, 2016), Indiana (SJR 14, 2016), Oklahoma (SJR 4,
  1 12 2016), and Louisiana (SCR 52, 2016),  for a convention for the
  1 13 specific and exclusive purpose of proposing amendments to the
  1 14 Constitution of the United States limited to the purposes
  1 15 stated therein, provided, however, that the delegates from
  1 16 Iowa to said convention are expressly limited to consideration
  1 17 and support of amendments that impose fiscal restraints on the
  1 18 federal government, and amendments that limit the power and
  1 19 jurisdiction of the federal government, and no amendments on
  1 20 any other topic; and
  1 21    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That it is the express intention of
  1 22 the General Assembly that this application shall be aggregated
  1 23 with the prior and subsequent applications of other states
  1 24 limited to the purposes identified in this application; and
  1 25    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That this application constitutes
  1 26 a continuing application in accordance with Article V of the
  1 27 Constitution of the United States until the legislatures of at
  1 28 least two=thirds of the several states have made applications
  1 29 for a similar convention under Article V, or the General
  1 30 Assembly resolves to withdraw this application; and
  1 31    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That the Secretary of State shall
  1 32 transmit certified copies of this resolution to the President
  1 33 and Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and
  1 34 Clerk of the United States House of Representatives, the
  1 35 presiding officer of each house of the legislature of each of
  2  1 the several states, and to each member of Iowa's congressional
  2  2 delegation.
  2  3                           EXPLANATION
  2  4 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  2  5 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  2  6    This joint resolution constitutes an application requesting
  2  7 the United States Congress to call a constitutional convention
  2  8 in order to propose amendments to the Constitution of the
  2  9 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 10 government and limit the power and jurisdiction of the federal
  2 11 government. The resolution stipulates that Iowa's delegates
  2 12 to such a convention are expressly limited to consideration
  2 13 and support of amendments on those topics. The resolution
  2 14 constitutes a continuing application to call a constitutional
  2 15 convention and states the intention of the General Assembly
  2 16 that the application be aggregated with the prior and
  2 17 subsequent applications of other states limited to the purposes
  2 18 identified in the resolution.
  2 19    The resolution also petitions the Congress of the United
  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.

 HOUSE JOINT RESOLUTION

  1 A Joint Resolution calling for an Article V convention in order
  2    to propose amendments to the Constitution of the United
  3    States that impose fiscal restraints, and limit the power
  4    and jurisdiction of the federal government, and requesting
  5    Congress to similarly propose such amendments.
  6 WHEREAS, the founders of the Constitution of the United
  7 States empowered state legislators to be guardians of liberty
  8 against future abuses of power by the federal government; and
  9 WHEREAS, the federal government has created a crushing
 10 national debt through improper and imprudent spending; and
 11 WHEREAS, the federal government has invaded the legitimate
 12 roles of the states through the manipulative process of federal
 13 mandates, most of which are unfunded to a great extent; and
 14 WHEREAS, the federal government has ceased to live under
 15 a proper interpretation of the Constitution of the United
 16 States; and
 17 WHEREAS, it is the solemn duty of the states to protect
 18 the liberty of our people, particularly for the generations
 19 to come, by proposing amendments to the Constitution of the
 20 United States through a convention of the states under Article
 21 V of the Constitution of the United States for the purpose of
 22 restraining these and related abuses of power; NOW THEREFORE,
 23 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE GENERAL ASSEMBLY OF THE STATE OF IOWA:
    TLSB 2105YH (5) 87
    aw/rj

PAG LIN

  2 15 convention and states the intention of the General Assembly
  2 16 that the application be aggregated with the prior and
  2 17 subsequent applications of other states limited to the purposes
  2 18 identified in the resolution.
  2 19    The resolution also petitions the Congress of the United
  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.

                                     GRASSLEY,
                                     BLOOMINGDALE, and
                                     ZUMBACH

 HOUSE JOINT RESOLUTION

  1 A Joint Resolution calling for an Article V convention in order
  2    to propose amendments to the Constitution of the United
  3    States that impose fiscal restraints, and limit the power
  4    and jurisdiction of the federal government, and requesting
  5    Congress to similarly propose such amendments.
  6 WHEREAS, the founders of the Constitution of the United
  7 States empowered state legislators to be guardians of liberty
  8 against future abuses of power by the federal government; and
  9 WHEREAS, the federal government has created a crushing
 10 national debt through improper and imprudent spending; and
 11 WHEREAS, the federal government has invaded the legitimate
 12 roles of the states through the manipulative process of federal
 13 mandates, most of which are unfunded to a great extent; and
 14 WHEREAS, the federal government has ceased to live under
 15 a proper interpretation of the Constitution of the United
 16 States; and
 17 WHEREAS, it is the solemn duty of the states to protect
 18 the liberty of our people, particularly for the generations
 19 to come, by proposing amendments to the Constitution of the
 20 United States through a convention of the states under Article
 21 V of the Constitution of the United States for the purpose of
 22 restraining these and related abuses of power; NOW THEREFORE,
 23 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE GENERAL ASSEMBLY OF THE STATE OF IOWA:
    TLSB 2105YH (5) 87
    aw/rj

PAG LIN



  1  1    That the Congress of the United States is hereby petitioned
  1  2 to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the United
  1  3 States, for submission to the states for ratification, to
  1  4 impose fiscal restraints on the federal government and limit
  1  5 the federal government's power and jurisdiction; and
  1  6    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That, pursuant to Article V of the
  1  7 Constitution of the United States, the General Assembly, as the
  1  8 legislature of the state of Iowa, joins in the applications of
  1  9 the states of Georgia (SR 736, 2014), Florida (SM 476, 2014),
  1 10 Alaska (HJR 22, 2014), Alabama (HJR 112, 2015), Tennessee
  1 11 (SJR 67, 2016), Indiana (SJR 14, 2016), Oklahoma (SJR 4,
  1 12 2016), and Louisiana (SCR 52, 2016),  for a convention for the
  1 13 specific and exclusive purpose of proposing amendments to the
  1 14 Constitution of the United States limited to the purposes
  1 15 stated therein, provided, however, that the delegates from
  1 16 Iowa to said convention are expressly limited to consideration
  1 17 and support of amendments that impose fiscal restraints on the
  1 18 federal government, and amendments that limit the power and
  1 19 jurisdiction of the federal government, and no amendments on
  1 20 any other topic; and
  1 21    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That it is the express intention of
  1 22 the General Assembly that this application shall be aggregated
  1 23 with the prior and subsequent applications of other states
  1 24 limited to the purposes identified in this application; and
  1 25    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That this application constitutes
  1 26 a continuing application in accordance with Article V of the
  1 27 Constitution of the United States until the legislatures of at
  1 28 least two=thirds of the several states have made applications
  1 29 for a similar convention under Article V, or the General
  1 30 Assembly resolves to withdraw this application; and
  1 31    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That the Secretary of State shall
  1 32 transmit certified copies of this resolution to the President
  1 33 and Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and
  1 34 Clerk of the United States House of Representatives, the
  1 35 presiding officer of each house of the legislature of each of
  2  1 the several states, and to each member of Iowa's congressional
  2  2 delegation.
  2  3                           EXPLANATION
  2  4 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  2  5 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  2  6    This joint resolution constitutes an application requesting
  2  7 the United States Congress to call a constitutional convention
  2  8 in order to propose amendments to the Constitution of the
  2  9 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 10 government and limit the power and jurisdiction of the federal
  2 11 government. The resolution stipulates that Iowa's delegates
  2 12 to such a convention are expressly limited to consideration
  2 13 and support of amendments on those topics. The resolution
  2 14 constitutes a continuing application to call a constitutional
  2 15 convention and states the intention of the General Assembly
  2 16 that the application be aggregated with the prior and
  2 17 subsequent applications of other states limited to the purposes
  2 18 identified in the resolution.
  2 19    The resolution also petitions the Congress of the United
  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.

  1 33 and Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and
  1 34 Clerk of the United States House of Representatives, the
  1 35 presiding officer of each house of the legislature of each of
  2  1 the several states, and to each member of Iowa's congressional
  2  2 delegation.
  2  3                           EXPLANATION
  2  4 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  2  5 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  2  6    This joint resolution constitutes an application requesting
  2  7 the United States Congress to call a constitutional convention
  2  8 in order to propose amendments to the Constitution of the
  2  9 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 10 government and limit the power and jurisdiction of the federal
  2 11 government. The resolution stipulates that Iowa's delegates
  2 12 to such a convention are expressly limited to consideration
  2 13 and support of amendments on those topics. The resolution
  2 14 constitutes a continuing application to call a constitutional
  2 15 convention and states the intention of the General Assembly
  2 16 that the application be aggregated with the prior and
  2 17 subsequent applications of other states limited to the purposes
  2 18 identified in the resolution.
  2 19    The resolution also petitions the Congress of the United
  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.
       LSB 2105YH (5) 87
       aw/rj
  1 A Joint Resolution calling for an Article V convention in order
  2    to propose amendments to the Constitution of the United
  3    States that impose fiscal restraints, and limit the power
  4    and jurisdiction of the federal government, and requesting
  5    Congress to similarly propose such amendments.
  6 WHEREAS, the founders of the Constitution of the United
  7 States empowered state legislators to be guardians of liberty
  8 against future abuses of power by the federal government; and
  9 WHEREAS, the federal government has created a crushing
 10 national debt through improper and imprudent spending; and
 11 WHEREAS, the federal government has invaded the legitimate
 12 roles of the states through the manipulative process of federal
 13 mandates, most of which are unfunded to a great extent; and
 14 WHEREAS, the federal government has ceased to live under
 15 a proper interpretation of the Constitution of the United
 16 States; and
 17 WHEREAS, it is the solemn duty of the states to protect
 18 the liberty of our people, particularly for the generations
 19 to come, by proposing amendments to the Constitution of the
 20 United States through a convention of the states under Article
 21 V of the Constitution of the United States for the purpose of
 22 restraining these and related abuses of power; NOW THEREFORE,
 23 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE GENERAL ASSEMBLY OF THE STATE OF IOWA:
    TLSB 2105YH (5) 87
    aw/rj

PAG LIN



  1  1    That the Congress of the United States is hereby petitioned
  1  2 to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the United
  1  3 States, for submission to the states for ratification, to
  1  4 impose fiscal restraints on the federal government and limit
  1  5 the federal government's power and jurisdiction; and
  1  6    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That, pursuant to Article V of the
  1  7 Constitution of the United States, the General Assembly, as the
  1  8 legislature of the state of Iowa, joins in the applications of
  1  9 the states of Georgia (SR 736, 2014), Florida (SM 476, 2014),
  1 10 Alaska (HJR 22, 2014), Alabama (HJR 112, 2015), Tennessee
  1 11 (SJR 67, 2016), Indiana (SJR 14, 2016), Oklahoma (SJR 4,
  1 12 2016), and Louisiana (SCR 52, 2016),  for a convention for the
  1 13 specific and exclusive purpose of proposing amendments to the
  1 14 Constitution of the United States limited to the purposes
  1 15 stated therein, provided, however, that the delegates from
  1 16 Iowa to said convention are expressly limited to consideration
  1 17 and support of amendments that impose fiscal restraints on the
  1 18 federal government, and amendments that limit the power and
  1 19 jurisdiction of the federal government, and no amendments on
  1 20 any other topic; and
  1 21    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That it is the express intention of
  1 22 the General Assembly that this application shall be aggregated
  1 23 with the prior and subsequent applications of other states
  1 24 limited to the purposes identified in this application; and
  1 25    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That this application constitutes
  1 26 a continuing application in accordance with Article V of the
  1 27 Constitution of the United States until the legislatures of at
  1 28 least two=thirds of the several states have made applications
  1 29 for a similar convention under Article V, or the General
  1 30 Assembly resolves to withdraw this application; and
  1 31    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That the Secretary of State shall
  1 32 transmit certified copies of this resolution to the President
  1 33 and Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and
  1 34 Clerk of the United States House of Representatives, the
  1 35 presiding officer of each house of the legislature of each of
  2  1 the several states, and to each member of Iowa's congressional
  2  2 delegation.

  2  2 delegation.
  2  3                           EXPLANATION
  2  4 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  2  5 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  2  6    This joint resolution constitutes an application requesting
  2  7 the United States Congress to call a constitutional convention
  2  8 in order to propose amendments to the Constitution of the
  2  9 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 10 government and limit the power and jurisdiction of the federal
  2 11 government. The resolution stipulates that Iowa's delegates
  2 12 to such a convention are expressly limited to consideration
  2 13 and support of amendments on those topics. The resolution
  2 14 constitutes a continuing application to call a constitutional
  2 15 convention and states the intention of the General Assembly
  2 16 that the application be aggregated with the prior and
  2 17 subsequent applications of other states limited to the purposes
  2 18 identified in the resolution.
  2 19    The resolution also petitions the Congress of the United
  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.
       LSB 2105YH (5) 87
       aw/rj
  7 States empowered state legislators to be guardians of liberty
  8 against future abuses of power by the federal government; and
  9 WHEREAS, the federal government has created a crushing
 10 national debt through improper and imprudent spending; and
 11 WHEREAS, the federal government has invaded the legitimate
 12 roles of the states through the manipulative process of federal
 13 mandates, most of which are unfunded to a great extent; and
 14 WHEREAS, the federal government has ceased to live under
 15 a proper interpretation of the Constitution of the United
 16 States; and
 17 WHEREAS, it is the solemn duty of the states to protect
 18 the liberty of our people, particularly for the generations
 19 to come, by proposing amendments to the Constitution of the
 20 United States through a convention of the states under Article
 21 V of the Constitution of the United States for the purpose of
 22 restraining these and related abuses of power; NOW THEREFORE,
 23 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE GENERAL ASSEMBLY OF THE STATE OF IOWA:

PAG LIN



  1  1    That the Congress of the United States is hereby petitioned
  1  2 to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the United
  1  3 States, for submission to the states for ratification, to
  1  4 impose fiscal restraints on the federal government and limit
  1  5 the federal government's power and jurisdiction; and
  1  6    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That, pursuant to Article V of the
  1  7 Constitution of the United States, the General Assembly, as the
  1  8 legislature of the state of Iowa, joins in the applications of
  1  9 the states of Georgia (SR 736, 2014), Florida (SM 476, 2014),
  1 10 Alaska (HJR 22, 2014), Alabama (HJR 112, 2015), Tennessee
  1 11 (SJR 67, 2016), Indiana (SJR 14, 2016), Oklahoma (SJR 4,
  1 12 2016), and Louisiana (SCR 52, 2016),  for a convention for the
  1 13 specific and exclusive purpose of proposing amendments to the
  1 14 Constitution of the United States limited to the purposes
  1 15 stated therein, provided, however, that the delegates from
  1 16 Iowa to said convention are expressly limited to consideration
  1 17 and support of amendments that impose fiscal restraints on the
  1 18 federal government, and amendments that limit the power and
  1 19 jurisdiction of the federal government, and no amendments on
  1 20 any other topic; and
  1 21    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That it is the express intention of
  1 22 the General Assembly that this application shall be aggregated
  1 23 with the prior and subsequent applications of other states
  1 24 limited to the purposes identified in this application; and
  1 25    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That this application constitutes
  1 26 a continuing application in accordance with Article V of the
  1 27 Constitution of the United States until the legislatures of at
  1 28 least two=thirds of the several states have made applications
  1 29 for a similar convention under Article V, or the General
  1 30 Assembly resolves to withdraw this application; and
  1 31    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That the Secretary of State shall
  1 32 transmit certified copies of this resolution to the President
  1 33 and Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and
  1 34 Clerk of the United States House of Representatives, the
  1 35 presiding officer of each house of the legislature of each of
  2  1 the several states, and to each member of Iowa's congressional
  2  2 delegation.

 23 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE GENERAL ASSEMBLY OF THE STATE OF IOWA:
    TLSB 2105YH (5) 87
    aw/rj

PAG LIN



  1  1    That the Congress of the United States is hereby petitioned
  1  2 to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the United
  1  3 States, for submission to the states for ratification, to
  1  4 impose fiscal restraints on the federal government and limit
  1  5 the federal government's power and jurisdiction; and
  1  6    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That, pursuant to Article V of the
  1  7 Constitution of the United States, the General Assembly, as the
  1  8 legislature of the state of Iowa, joins in the applications of
  1  9 the states of Georgia (SR 736, 2014), Florida (SM 476, 2014),
  1 10 Alaska (HJR 22, 2014), Alabama (HJR 112, 2015), Tennessee
  1 11 (SJR 67, 2016), Indiana (SJR 14, 2016), Oklahoma (SJR 4,
  1 12 2016), and Louisiana (SCR 52, 2016),  for a convention for the
  1 13 specific and exclusive purpose of proposing amendments to the
  1 14 Constitution of the United States limited to the purposes
  1 15 stated therein, provided, however, that the delegates from
  1 16 Iowa to said convention are expressly limited to consideration
  1 17 and support of amendments that impose fiscal restraints on the
  1 18 federal government, and amendments that limit the power and
  1 19 jurisdiction of the federal government, and no amendments on
  1 20 any other topic; and
  1 21    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That it is the express intention of
  1 22 the General Assembly that this application shall be aggregated
  1 23 with the prior and subsequent applications of other states
  1 24 limited to the purposes identified in this application; and
  1 25    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That this application constitutes
  1 26 a continuing application in accordance with Article V of the
  1 27 Constitution of the United States until the legislatures of at
  1 28 least two=thirds of the several states have made applications
  1 29 for a similar convention under Article V, or the General
  1 30 Assembly resolves to withdraw this application; and
  1 31    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That the Secretary of State shall
  1 32 transmit certified copies of this resolution to the President
  1 33 and Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and
  1 34 Clerk of the United States House of Representatives, the
  1 35 presiding officer of each house of the legislature of each of
  2  1 the several states, and to each member of Iowa's congressional
  2  2 delegation.
  2  3                           EXPLANATION
  2  4 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  2  5 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  2  6    This joint resolution constitutes an application requesting
  2  7 the United States Congress to call a constitutional convention
  2  8 in order to propose amendments to the Constitution of the
  2  9 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 10 government and limit the power and jurisdiction of the federal
  2 11 government. The resolution stipulates that Iowa's delegates
  2 12 to such a convention are expressly limited to consideration
  2 13 and support of amendments on those topics. The resolution
  2 14 constitutes a continuing application to call a constitutional
  2 15 convention and states the intention of the General Assembly
  2 16 that the application be aggregated with the prior and
  2 17 subsequent applications of other states limited to the purposes
  2 18 identified in the resolution.
  2 19    The resolution also petitions the Congress of the United
  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.

    TLSB 2105YH (5) 87
    aw/rj

PAG LIN



  1  1    That the Congress of the United States is hereby petitioned
  1  2 to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the United
  1  3 States, for submission to the states for ratification, to
  1  4 impose fiscal restraints on the federal government and limit
  1  5 the federal government's power and jurisdiction; and
  1  6    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That, pursuant to Article V of the
  1  7 Constitution of the United States, the General Assembly, as the
  1  8 legislature of the state of Iowa, joins in the applications of
  1  9 the states of Georgia (SR 736, 2014), Florida (SM 476, 2014),
  1 10 Alaska (HJR 22, 2014), Alabama (HJR 112, 2015), Tennessee
  1 11 (SJR 67, 2016), Indiana (SJR 14, 2016), Oklahoma (SJR 4,
  1 12 2016), and Louisiana (SCR 52, 2016),  for a convention for the
  1 13 specific and exclusive purpose of proposing amendments to the
  1 14 Constitution of the United States limited to the purposes
  1 15 stated therein, provided, however, that the delegates from
  1 16 Iowa to said convention are expressly limited to consideration
  1 17 and support of amendments that impose fiscal restraints on the
  1 18 federal government, and amendments that limit the power and
  1 19 jurisdiction of the federal government, and no amendments on
  1 20 any other topic; and
  1 21    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That it is the express intention of
  1 22 the General Assembly that this application shall be aggregated
  1 23 with the prior and subsequent applications of other states
  1 24 limited to the purposes identified in this application; and
  1 25    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That this application constitutes
  1 26 a continuing application in accordance with Article V of the
  1 27 Constitution of the United States until the legislatures of at
  1 28 least two=thirds of the several states have made applications
  1 29 for a similar convention under Article V, or the General
  1 30 Assembly resolves to withdraw this application; and
  1 31    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That the Secretary of State shall
  1 32 transmit certified copies of this resolution to the President
  1 33 and Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and
  1 34 Clerk of the United States House of Representatives, the
  1 35 presiding officer of each house of the legislature of each of
  2  1 the several states, and to each member of Iowa's congressional
  2  2 delegation.
  2  3                           EXPLANATION
  2  4 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  2  5 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  2  6    This joint resolution constitutes an application requesting
  2  7 the United States Congress to call a constitutional convention
  2  8 in order to propose amendments to the Constitution of the
  2  9 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 10 government and limit the power and jurisdiction of the federal
  2 11 government. The resolution stipulates that Iowa's delegates
  2 12 to such a convention are expressly limited to consideration
  2 13 and support of amendments on those topics. The resolution
  2 14 constitutes a continuing application to call a constitutional
  2 15 convention and states the intention of the General Assembly
  2 16 that the application be aggregated with the prior and
  2 17 subsequent applications of other states limited to the purposes
  2 18 identified in the resolution.
  2 19    The resolution also petitions the Congress of the United
  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.

  2  7 the United States Congress to call a constitutional convention
  2  8 in order to propose amendments to the Constitution of the
  2  9 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 10 government and limit the power and jurisdiction of the federal
  2 11 government. The resolution stipulates that Iowa's delegates
  2 12 to such a convention are expressly limited to consideration
  2 13 and support of amendments on those topics. The resolution
  2 14 constitutes a continuing application to call a constitutional
  2 15 convention and states the intention of the General Assembly
  2 16 that the application be aggregated with the prior and
  2 17 subsequent applications of other states limited to the purposes
  2 18 identified in the resolution.
  2 19    The resolution also petitions the Congress of the United
  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.
       LSB 2105YH (5) 87
       aw/rj
  1  1    That the Congress of the United States is hereby petitioned
  1  2 to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the United
  1  3 States, for submission to the states for ratification, to
  1  4 impose fiscal restraints on the federal government and limit
  1  5 the federal government's power and jurisdiction; and
  1  6    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That, pursuant to Article V of the
  1  7 Constitution of the United States, the General Assembly, as the
  1  8 legislature of the state of Iowa, joins in the applications of
  1  9 the states of Georgia (SR 736, 2014), Florida (SM 476, 2014),
  1 10 Alaska (HJR 22, 2014), Alabama (HJR 112, 2015), Tennessee
  1 11 (SJR 67, 2016), Indiana (SJR 14, 2016), Oklahoma (SJR 4,
  1 12 2016), and Louisiana (SCR 52, 2016),  for a convention for the
  1 13 specific and exclusive purpose of proposing amendments to the
  1 14 Constitution of the United States limited to the purposes
  1 15 stated therein, provided, however, that the delegates from
  1 16 Iowa to said convention are expressly limited to consideration
  1 17 and support of amendments that impose fiscal restraints on the
  1 18 federal government, and amendments that limit the power and
  1 19 jurisdiction of the federal government, and no amendments on
  1 20 any other topic; and
  1 21    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That it is the express intention of
  1 22 the General Assembly that this application shall be aggregated
  1 23 with the prior and subsequent applications of other states
  1 24 limited to the purposes identified in this application; and
  1 25    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That this application constitutes
  1 26 a continuing application in accordance with Article V of the
  1 27 Constitution of the United States until the legislatures of at
  1 28 least two=thirds of the several states have made applications
  1 29 for a similar convention under Article V, or the General
  1 30 Assembly resolves to withdraw this application; and
  1 31    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That the Secretary of State shall
  1 32 transmit certified copies of this resolution to the President
  1 33 and Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and
  1 34 Clerk of the United States House of Representatives, the
  1 35 presiding officer of each house of the legislature of each of
  2  1 the several states, and to each member of Iowa's congressional
  2  2 delegation.

  1 11 (SJR 67, 2016), Indiana (SJR 14, 2016), Oklahoma (SJR 4,
  1 12 2016), and Louisiana (SCR 52, 2016),  for a convention for the
  1 13 specific and exclusive purpose of proposing amendments to the
  1 14 Constitution of the United States limited to the purposes
  1 15 stated therein, provided, however, that the delegates from
  1 16 Iowa to said convention are expressly limited to consideration
  1 17 and support of amendments that impose fiscal restraints on the
  1 18 federal government, and amendments that limit the power and
  1 19 jurisdiction of the federal government, and no amendments on
  1 20 any other topic; and
  1 21    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That it is the express intention of
  1 22 the General Assembly that this application shall be aggregated
  1 23 with the prior and subsequent applications of other states
  1 24 limited to the purposes identified in this application; and
  1 25    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That this application constitutes
  1 26 a continuing application in accordance with Article V of the
  1 27 Constitution of the United States until the legislatures of at
  1 28 least two=thirds of the several states have made applications
  1 29 for a similar convention under Article V, or the General
  1 30 Assembly resolves to withdraw this application; and
  1 31    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That the Secretary of State shall
  1 32 transmit certified copies of this resolution to the President
  1 33 and Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and
  1 34 Clerk of the United States House of Representatives, the
  1 35 presiding officer of each house of the legislature of each of
  2  1 the several states, and to each member of Iowa's congressional
  2  2 delegation.
  2  3                           EXPLANATION
  2  4 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  2  5 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  2  6    This joint resolution constitutes an application requesting
  2  7 the United States Congress to call a constitutional convention
  2  8 in order to propose amendments to the Constitution of the
  2  9 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 10 government and limit the power and jurisdiction of the federal
  2 11 government. The resolution stipulates that Iowa's delegates
  2 12 to such a convention are expressly limited to consideration
  2 13 and support of amendments on those topics. The resolution
  2 14 constitutes a continuing application to call a constitutional
  2 15 convention and states the intention of the General Assembly
  2 16 that the application be aggregated with the prior and
  2 17 subsequent applications of other states limited to the purposes
  2 18 identified in the resolution.
  2 19    The resolution also petitions the Congress of the United
  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.

  2  3                           EXPLANATION
  2  4 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  2  5 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  2  6    This joint resolution constitutes an application requesting
  2  7 the United States Congress to call a constitutional convention
  2  8 in order to propose amendments to the Constitution of the
  2  9 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 10 government and limit the power and jurisdiction of the federal
  2 11 government. The resolution stipulates that Iowa's delegates
  2 12 to such a convention are expressly limited to consideration
  2 13 and support of amendments on those topics. The resolution
  2 14 constitutes a continuing application to call a constitutional
  2 15 convention and states the intention of the General Assembly
  2 16 that the application be aggregated with the prior and
  2 17 subsequent applications of other states limited to the purposes
  2 18 identified in the resolution.
  2 19    The resolution also petitions the Congress of the United
  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.
       LSB 2105YH (5) 87
       aw/rj
  1 20 any other topic; and
  1 21    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That it is the express intention of
  1 22 the General Assembly that this application shall be aggregated
  1 23 with the prior and subsequent applications of other states
  1 24 limited to the purposes identified in this application; and
  1 25    BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, That this application constitutes
  1 26 a continuing application in accordance with Article V of the
  1 27 Constitution of the United States until the legislatures of at
  1 28 least two=thirds of the several states have made applications
  1 29 for a similar convention under Article V, or the General
  1 30 Assembly resolves to withdraw this application; and

  1 32 transmit certified copies of this resolution to the President

  1 33 and Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and

  2  3                           EXPLANATION
  2  4 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  2  5 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  2  6    This joint resolution constitutes an application requesting
  2  7 the United States Congress to call a constitutional convention
  2  8 in order to propose amendments to the Constitution of the
  2  9 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 10 government and limit the power and jurisdiction of the federal
  2 11 government. The resolution stipulates that Iowa's delegates
  2 12 to such a convention are expressly limited to consideration
  2 13 and support of amendments on those topics. The resolution
  2 14 constitutes a continuing application to call a constitutional
  2 15 convention and states the intention of the General Assembly
  2 16 that the application be aggregated with the prior and
  2 17 subsequent applications of other states limited to the purposes
  2 18 identified in the resolution.
  2 19    The resolution also petitions the Congress of the United
  2 20 States to propose an amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 21 United States to impose fiscal restraints on the federal
  2 22 government and limit the federal government's power and
  2 23 jurisdiction.
  2 24    The resolution requires the Secretary of State to transmit
  2 25 certified copies of this resolution to the President and
  2 26 Secretary of the United States Senate, the Speaker and Clerk
  2 27 of the United States House of Representatives, the presiding
  2 28 officer of each house of the legislature of each state, and to
  2 29 the members of Iowa's congressional delegation.
       LSB 2105YH (5) 87

  2  2 delegation.
